        </div><div class="casAbstract">Fe oxides are very promising anode materials based on conversion reactions for Li-ion batteries (LIBs).  During conversion processes, the crystal structure and compn. of the electrode material are drastically changed.  Surprisingly, inheritance of a crystallog. orientation was found during lithiation/delithiation processes of single-crystal α-Fe2O3 nanocubes by ex situ TEM.  Single-crystal α-Fe2O3 was 1st transformed into numerous Fe nanograins embedded in a Li2O matrix, and then the conversion between Fe and FeO nanograins became the main reversible electrochem. reaction for energy storage.  These Fe/FeO nanograins had almost the same crystallog. orientation, indicating that the lithiated/delithiated products can inherit the crystallog. orientation of single-crystal α-Fe2O3.  This finding is important for understanding the detailed electrochem. conversion processes of Fe oxides, and this feature may also exist during lithiation/delithiation processes of other transition-metal oxides.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGoVbdA4fBwFg7Vg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lhPVPDdp6wQ7w"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2MXhs1ChtrrN&amp;md5=445590177fff5f17a5693d7051277d03</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref49"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref49" class="rightTabRefNumLink">49</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit49" data-doi="10.1103/PhysRevLett.97.187401"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Ferrari, A. C.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Meyer, J. C.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Scardaci, V.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Casiraghi, C.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Lazzeri, M.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Mauri, F.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Piscanec, S.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Jiang, D.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Novoselov, K. S.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Roth, S.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Geim, A. K.</span><span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Raman Spectrum of Graphene and Graphene Layers</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Phys. Rev. Lett.</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2006</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">97</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">187401</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1103/PhysRevLett.97.187401</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit49R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">49</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Raman Spectrum of Graphene and Graphene Layers</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Ferrari, A. C.; Meyer, J. C.; Scardaci, V.; Casiraghi, C.; Lazzeri, M.; Mauri, F.; Piscanec, S.; Jiang, D.; Novoselov, K. S.; Roth, S.; Geim, A. K.</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Physical Review Letters</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2006</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">97</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">18</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">187401/1-187401/4</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">PRLTAO</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">0031-9007</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">American Physical Society</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Graphene is the 2-dimensional building block for C allotropes of every other dimensionality.  Its electronic structure is captured in its Raman spectrum that clearly evolves with the no. of layers.  The D peak 2nd order changes in shape, width, and position for an increasing no. of layers, reflecting the change in the electron bands via a double resonant Raman process.  The G peak slightly down-shifts.  This allows unambiguous, high-throughput, nondestructive identification of graphene layers, which is critically lacking in this emerging research area.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGo35CDycv0LILVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lhPVPDdp6wQ7w"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BD28XhtFKqtbvP&amp;md5=8b1d9f77f616aea008d55ba4fbb3f0bb</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref50"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref50" class="rightTabRefNumLink">50</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit50" data-doi="10.1021/la804216z"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Paredes, J. I.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Villar-Rodil, S.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Solís-Fernández, P.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Martínez-Alonso, A.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Tascón, J. M. D.</span><span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Atomic Force and Scanning Tunneling Microscopy Imaging of Graphene Nanosheets Derived from Graphite Oxide</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Langmuir</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2009</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">25</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">5957</span><span class="NLM_x">–</span> <span class="NLM_lpage">5968</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1021/la804216z</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit50R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">50</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Atomic Force and Scanning Tunneling Microscopy Imaging of Graphene Nanosheets Derived from Graphite Oxide</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Paredes, J. I.; Villar-Rodil, S.; Solis-Fernandez, P.; Martinez-Alonso, A.; Tascon, J. M. D.</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Langmuir</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2009</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">25</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">10</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">5957-5968</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">LANGD5</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">0743-7463</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">American Chemical Society</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Graphene nanosheets produced in the form of stable aq. dispersions by chem. redn. of graphene oxide and deposited onto graphite substrates have been investigated by at. force and scanning tunneling microscopy (AFM/STM).  The chem. reduced graphene oxide nanosheets were hardly distinguishable from their unreduced counterparts in the topog. AFM images.  However, they could be readily discriminated through phase imaging in the attractive regime of tapping-mode AFM, probably because of differences in hydrophilicity arising from their distinct oxygen contents.  The chem. reduced nanosheets displayed a smoothly undulated, globular morphol. on the nanometer scale, with typical vertical variations in the subnanometer range and lateral feature sizes of ∼5-10 nm.  Such morphol. was attributed to be the result of significant structural disorder in the carbon skeleton, which originates during the strong oxidn. that leads to graphene oxide and remains after chem. redn.  Direct evidence of structural disorder was provided by at.-scale STM imaging, which revealed an absence of long-range periodicity in the graphene nanosheets.  Only structured domains a few nanometers large were obsd. instead.  Likewise, the nanosheet edges appeared atomically rough and ill-defined, though smooth on the nanometer scale.  The unreduced graphene oxide nanosheets could only be imaged by STM at very low tunneling currents (∼1 pA), being visualized in some cases with inverted contrast relative to the graphite substrate, a result that was attributed to their extremely low cond.  Complementary characterization of the unreduced and chem. reduced nanosheets was carried out by thermogravimetric anal. as well as UV-visible absorption and X-ray photoelectron and Raman spectroscopies.  In particular, the somewhat puzzling Raman results were interpreted to be the result of an amorphous character of the graphene oxide material.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGqP3DAIGzG4DLVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lhPVPDdp6wQ7w"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BD1MXjvF2gtrY%253D&amp;md5=003680ec80967b1e6606a3bd8e35de3c</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref51"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref51" class="rightTabRefNumLink">51</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit51" data-doi="10.1016/j.carbon.2007.02.034"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Stankovich, S.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Dikin, D. A.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Piner, R. D.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Kohlhaas, K. A.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Kleinhammes, A.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Jia, Y.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Wu, Y.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Nguyen, S. T.</span><span class="NLM_x">; </span><span class="NLM_contrib-group">Ruoff, R. S.</span><span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Synthesis of Graphene-Based Nanosheets via Chemical Reduction of Exfoliated Graphite Oxide</span> <span class="citation_source-journal">Carbon</span><span class="NLM_x"> </span><span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2007</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_volume">45</span><span class="NLM_x">, </span> <span class="NLM_fpage">1558</span><span class="NLM_x">–</span> <span class="NLM_lpage">1565</span><span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1016/j.carbon.2007.02.034</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit51R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">51</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Synthesis of graphene-based nanosheets via chemical reduction of exfoliated graphite oxide</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Stankovich, Sasha; Dikin, Dmitriy A.; Piner, Richard D.; Kohlhaas, Kevin A.; Kleinhammes, Alfred; Jia, Yuanyuan; Wu, Yue; Nguyen, SonBinh T.; Ruoff, Rodney S.</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Carbon</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2007</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">45</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">7</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">1558-1565</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">CRBNAH</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">0008-6223</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Elsevier Ltd.</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Redn. of a colloidal suspension of exfoliated graphene oxide sheets in water with hydrazine hydrate results in their aggregation and subsequent formation of a high-surface-area carbon material which consists of thin graphene-based sheets.  The reduced material was characterized by elemental anal., thermogravimetric anal., SEM, XPS, NMR spectroscopy, Raman spectroscopy, and elec. cond. measurements.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGrrhZ_RTUhlnLVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lhPVPDdp6wQ7w"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BD2sXmtVGkur4%253D&amp;md5=23435c3ac8a9c1ac250e189651040248</span></div></div></div></div></li></ol></li><li id="pane-m3" aria-labelledby="pane-m3" class="tab__pane tab__pane-suppInfo"><h2 class="supp-info-label">Supporting Information</h2><div class="article_supporting-info" id="rightTab-notes-1"><div class="article_content-header"><div class="article_content-header-row"><div class="article_content-title" tabindex="0"><h2 id="rightTab-_i9">Supporting Information</h2></div></div></div><hr><p class="last">The Supporting Information is available free of charge on the <a href="/" class="ext-link">ACS Publications website</a> at DOI: <a href="/doi/abs/10.1021/acsami.7b04407" class="ext-link">10.1021/acsami.7b04407</a>.</p><ul class="NLM_list-list_type-label" id="silist"><li><p class="inline">TEM image and SAED pattern of pure Fe<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub> crystals, discharge/charge profiles of the Fe<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>/rGO, pure rGO, and pure Fe<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub> electrodes, cycling performance of the pure rGO electrode, and rate capability of the pure rGO electrode (<a href="/doi/suppl/10.1021/acsami.7b04407/suppl_file/am7b04407_si_001.pdf" class="ext-link">PDF</a>)</p></li></ul><p></p><div class="supInfoBoxOnFTP "><div class="sup-info-attachments"><ul><li><a class="suppl-anchor" href="/doi/suppl/10.1021/acsami.7b04407/suppl_file/am7b04407_si_001.pdf">am7b04407_si_001.pdf (1.04 MB)</a></li></ul></div></div><div id="rightTab-figshare-widget"></div><br><div class="TermsAndConditionsDropzoneRight" data-pb-dropzone="TermsAndConditionsDropzoneRight"><div data-widget-def="UX3HTMLWidget" data-widget-id="b84e6b6c-b4d0-4427-b286-3cf14d52d013" class="mb-4">

	    gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':'Main'});

	});


	$('.cit-download-dropdown_content ul li').on('click',function(e)
	{	
	//	e.preventDefault();
	    var idx = $(this).index();
	    
	    var label = '';
	    if (idx === 0 ) {
	    	label = 'Citation';
	    } else if (idx === 1 ) {
	    	label = 'Abstract';
	    } else if (idx === 2 ) {
	    	label = 'Reference';
	    } else if (idx === 3 ) {
	    	label = 'More Options';
	    }
	   
	   gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':label});
	});

	$('.header_contnav-next a').on('click', function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Right Arrow'});
	}); 

 	$('.header_contnav-pre a').on('click', function(e){
	    e.preventDefault();
	     gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Left Arrow'});
	});

		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Share'});
	});

	});

	});

<script nonce="90da8d1fa8b4b325-SJC">
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(){
    // Function to get a Human readable formatted date
    function getFormattedDateForMaintenance() {
        let today = new Date();
        let dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        //January is 0
        let mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0'); 
        let yyyy = today.getFullYear();
        
        let daysOfWeek = ['Sunday', 'Monday', 'Tuesday', 'Wednesday', 'Thursday', 'Friday', 'Saturday'];
        let monthsOfYear = ['January', 'February', 'March', 'April', 'May', 'June', 'July', 'August', 'September', 'October', 'November', 'December'];

        let dayOfWeek = daysOfWeek[today.getDay()];
        let monthOfYear = monthsOfYear[today.getMonth()];

        return dayOfWeek + ', ' + monthOfYear + ' ' + dd + ', ' + yyyy;
    }
    
    // Insert the date into the .system-message-date element
    document.querySelector('.system-message-date').innerText = getFormattedDateForMaintenance();
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" nonce="90da8d1fa8b4b325-SJC">

	/*

var infoCentralCapture = (function() {

    //Detect mobile device
    window.mobilecheck = function() {

        (function(a){if(/(android|bb\d+|meego).+mobile|avantgo|bada\/|blackberry|blazer|compal|elaine|fennec|hiptop|iemobile|ip(hone|od)|iris|kindle|lge |maemo|midp|mmp|mobile.+firefox|netfront|opera u|g560|gene|gf\-5|g\-mo|go(\.w|od)|gr(ad|un)|haie|hcit|hd\-(m|p|t)|hei\-|hi(pt|ta)|hp( i|ip)|hs\-c|ht(c(\-| |_|a|g|p|s|t)|tp)|hu(aw|tc)|i\-(20|go|ma)|i230|iac( |\-|\/)|ibro|idea|ig01|ikom|im1k|inno|ipaq|iris|ja(t|v)a|jbro|jemu|jigs|kddi|keji|kgt( |\/)|klon|kpt |kwc\-|kyo(c|k)|le(no|xi)|lg( g|\/(k|l|u)|50|54|\-[a-w])|libw|lynx|m1\-w|m3ga|m50\/|ma(te|ui|xo)|mc(01|21|ca)|m\-cr|me(rc|ri)|mi(o8|oa|ts)|mmef|mo(01|02|bi|de|do|t(\-| |o|v)|zz)|mt(50|p1|v )|mwbp|mywa|n10[0-2]|n20[2-3]|n30(0|2)|n50(0|2|5)|n7(0(0|1)|10)|ne((c|m)\-|on|tf|wf|wg|wt)|nok(6|i)|nzph|o2im|op(ti|wv)|oran|owg1|p800|pan(a|d|t)|pdxg|pg(13|\-([1-8]|c))|phil|pire|pl(ay|uc)|pn\-2|po(ck|rt|se)|prox|psio|pt\-g|qa\-a|qc(07|12|21|32|60|\-[2-7]|i\-)|qtek|r380|r600|raks|rim9|ro(ve|zo)|s55\/|sa(ge|ma|mm|ms|ny|va)|sc(01|h\-|oo|p\-)|sdk\/|se(c(\-|0|1)|47|mc|nd|ri)|sgh\-|shar|sie(\-|m)|sk\-0|sl(45|id)|sm(al|ar|b3|it|t5)|so(ft|ny)|sp(01|h\-|v\-|v )|sy(01|mb)|t2(18|50)|t6(00|10|18)|ta(gt|lk)|tcl\-|tdg\-|tel(i|m)|tim\-|t\-mo|to(pl|sh)|ts(70|m\-|m3|m5)|tx\-9|up(\.b|g1|si)|utst|v400|v750|veri|vi(rg|te)|vk(40|5[0-3]|\-v)|vm40|voda|vulc|vx(52|53|60|61|70|80|81|83|85|98)|w3c(\-| )|webc|whit|wi(g |nc|nw)|wmlb|wonu|x700|yas\-|your|zeto|zte\-/i.test(a.substr(0,4))) check = true;})(navigator.userAgent||navigator.vendor||window.opera);
              return check;
        };

    var _isMobile = window.mobilecheck();
    if (_isMobile) {
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').addClass('mobile');
    }

    var emailValid = "",
        time = 3000,
        btnStatus = true,
        errorStatus = false,
        errormessage = "<p class='gdpr_err'><b>Please Enter a valid email address<b><p>";

    function init() {
        setTimeout(function() {
            var cookieExist = getCookie("gdpr");
            if (cookieExist) {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie exist");
                return false;
            } else {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie does not exist")
                gdprMessage();
            }
            //Events
            $('#closebtn').on("click", hideForm);

            //Handle submit
            $('#gdpr-message-btn').on("click", function(event) {
                handleClick();
            });

            // //Hide if clicked outside div - TO DO stop handling click after submit
            // $(document).click(function(event) {
            // 	event.stopPropagation();
            //   console.log(event.target);
            //   if (!$(event.target).closest("#gdpr-message-content").length) {
            //     $("body").find("#gdpr-message-modal").hide();
            //     $(this).off();
            //   }
            // });
            $('#gdpr-con-btn').click(function() {
                setCookie("gdpr", "true");
                hideForm();
            });
        }, time);
    }

    //Show the message
    function gdprMessage() {
        //console.log("Show GDPR Message");
        var tMessage, emailInput, messageButton, ewrap;

        $('#gdpr-message-modal').show();
    }

    function handleClick() {
        //console.log($("#gdpr-input").val());
        emailValid = validateEmail($("#gdpr-input").val());
        if (emailValid) {
            //Submit the form
            //Hide form
            if ($('.gdpr_err')) {
                $('.gdpr_err').hide();
            }

            $("#gdpr-message-content")
                //If successful then...
            setCookie("gdpr", "true");
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid + " submiting form");
        } else {
            //Show error message
            gdprErrorMessage();
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid);
        }
    }

    function gdprErrorMessage() {
        if (errorStatus) {
            return false;
        } else {
            errorStatus = true;
            $("#gdpr-message-content").append(errormessage);
        }
    }

    function validateEmail(email) {
        var re = /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
        return re.test(String(email).toLowerCase());
    }

    function setCookie(name, value) {
        var expires = "";
        expires = "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
        document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
    }

    function getCookie(name) {
        var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(name + '=([^;]+)'));
        if (match) return match[1];
    }

    function hideForm() { //And set cookie
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').hide();
        setCookie("gdpr", "false");
        gtag('event', 'GDPR Modal', { 'event_category': 'Pubs GDPR', 'event_label':'GDPR Dismissal'});
    }

    return {
        init: init
    }
})();

$(document).ready(infoCentralCapture.init);
</script>


                    
                        



        
        <script nonce="90da8d1fa8b4b325-SJC">
var currentJournal = "ACS Applied Materials &amp;amp; Interfaces";
$(".citationLinks > a").click(function(e){
    if($(this).text() === "ACS Full Text ") {
        gtag('event', 'ACS Full Text', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Crossref") {
        gtag('event', 'Crossref', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "CAS") {
        gtag('event', 'CAS', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "PubMed") {
        gtag('event', 'PubMed', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Google Scholar") {
        gtag('event', 'Google Scholar', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).hasClass("issue-item_open-url") === true) {
        gtag('event', 'OpenURL', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
});
</script>

                    
                        



        
        <script nonce="90da8d1fa8b4b325-SJC">
$(document).ready(function(){
    var cookie = "";
    var uri = "/doi/full/10.1021/html_original_uri?id=123";
    console.log("ACSPubs2 start");
    $.getJSON('https://extreme-ip-lookup.com/json/', function(data, status) {
            if ( status == 'success' ) {
                $.each(data, function(i, field){
                    cookie=cookie.concat(i+' = '+field+" - ");
                });
                
            } else {
                    cookie=status;
            }

            cookie1 = cookie;
            cookie = cookie1 + "; path=/; domain=.acs.org";
            //document.cookie = "ACSPubs2= "+ btoa(cookie) ;
            $.cookie("ACSPubs2", btoa(cookie), {path: '/'}); // Session cookie valid across the entire site.
            //TODO send cookie val to the controller for logging
            console.log("ACSPubs2 success");
    })
    .fail(function(xx, status, err){
        cookie="error: 127.0.0.1";
        //document.cookie = "ACSPubs2= "+ btoa(cookie) ;
        $.cookie("ACSPubs2", btoa(cookie), {path: '/'}); // Session cookie valid across the entire site.
        console.log("ACSPubs2 failed");
        //TODO send cookie val to the controller for logging
    });
});    
</script>
